'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:
            i += 1
    return nums

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:
            i += 1
    return nums

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:
            i += 1
    return nums

def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()

        else:

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:
            i += 1
    return nums

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''

    while i < len(nums):

            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:

'''Write a python function to remove duplicate numbers from a given number of lists.'''
def removeDuplicates(nums):
    '''
    :param nums: list of numbers
    :return: list of numbers without duplicates
    '''
    nums.sort()
    i = 0
    while i < len(nums):
        if nums[i] == nums[i+1]:
            nums.pop(i+1)
        else:
            i += 1
    return nums
